name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Deluxe twin beds room with Chongqing' s night view
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:It was a disappointing stay. I went there for the name of Ramada, but what I got was the experience of a mid-to-low-end express hotel. I booked a twin room with night view in Anlan, Fog City, because of the night view pictures on Ctrip. I specifically told the front desk to ask for a high floor, because it was already night when I arrived in Chongqing. When I got the room card and opened the door, I saw a whole wall of floor-to-ceiling curtains. I couldn't wait to open the curtains, revealing a small window about one meter wide, and the rest was a solid wall. Yes, it's called comfort curtains. You can imagine that it is a large floor-to-ceiling curtain when you pull it up, but the view is less than 90 degrees and the view is a noisy main road. The expected night view of Chongqing was thus lost. I asked the front desk and they said that this room type is facing this direction. Well, if you can't ask for it outside, let's ask for it inside. As for the decoration, there is an induction cooker and a sink and a small range hood at the entrance. The floor is tile + cheap wooden floor. The bathroom is so cramped that it can only accommodate one person, and you have to turn sideways to open and close the door. Does this configuration and style look familiar to you? Yes, this is an apar**ent, which may have been converted into a hotel later. I lowered my expectations and didn't ask for luxury. I wanted something practical. But I have to mention a few complaints. The bed is 1.2 meters and an adult needs to sleep comfortably. The water from the faucet is small, especially when taking a shower, the hot water is slow and small. When the air conditioner is turned on, a musty smell permeates the room... The breakfast is very bad. For example, there is basically no decent meat in the noodles and sauce, all vegetables... The few kinds of Western pastries may be purchased from outside and taste bad. In short, Ramada Encore is really hard to be encore.

msg:我住華美達應該常客了，每月都會有幾次，一直都是好評 但是今天我一定會會給它一個差評並且用元寶不會再次入住。因為我的酒店訂單明天才退房，這次評價借的上次入住的訂單評價的，但是問題發生在今天7月30日晚。今晚回來乘坐高區4號電梯上26樓，電梯到了7樓的時候往下墜，是的你沒聽錯是往下掉了。掉到6樓的時候剎住了，一直在6，7樓徘徊了一會，我們驚魂稍定就趕緊按通話鍵給家酒店説電梯出了問題，一邊説一邊電梯開始哈恢復了往上走一直走到14樓停了。我們趕緊出來並告訴了準備乘電梯上行的住客電梯有問題，然後大家一起乘坐低區電梯到2樓換乘另外一部高區電梯。我就去前台告知電梯問題，讓他們儘快停止4號梯檢修，不然怕另外的住客也會出現問題，結果居然前台小哥居然一臉公事公辦的表情説知道了會反饋上次。媽的，我不喜歡説臟話，但是切實不得不説，這可是電梯下墜，運氣不好我們可能就掛了，而且後面的乘客也會有這個風險，居然不馬上去封鎖電梯還一臉無所謂的樣子，我是不知道他們的應急安全培訓是怎麼做的。更扯的事我在反饋這個問題給前台小哥的時候，他領導應該也在，也是一個小哥，估計是大堂經理，然後給他説別大聲説，等會去看看。**的你別聲張我能理解，不引起恐慌嘛，但是這種事你應該馬上安排人去看啊，而且應該馬上去把電梯停下來啊，要知道那可是到26樓的電梯，萬一高點出問題那就衹有全村吃席了。最後，強烈建議應急管理局來督促一下安全意識培訓。
